## 2025-08-14T14:04:05.506000Z â€” user
Mothball, Idle, and Surrender Sites
What are Mothball/Idle Sites?

â€œIdle sitesâ€ is an umbrella term that refers to sites originally in development, but which are no longer planned to be operational. â€œMothballâ€ sites are still intended for operations, but are paused after substantial completion and put on hold until a later date. Amazon is still liable to protect these buildingsâ€™ assets (HVAC, life safety systems, etc.), which necessitates installation of specially-configured BMS systems. The stage of IT connectivity per site determines the BMS configuration required to monitor.

To address this challenge, several business units have launched Idle Asset Planning (IAP) and Asset Retirement programs. # Eagle Eye â†’ Autologging Workflow (Pilot-ready)

**Goal:** Zero-interruption documentation. Techs do the work; cameras + systems draft the record. Techs only *review & correct* at dayâ€™s end (â‰¤3 min/job).

## How it works
1. **Auto-link cameras to assets**

   - Maintain a map: *Camera X* â†” *Asset IDs* â†” *Location/Line*.

   - If a tech **scans the asset tag** when arriving, start/extend the capture window.

   - Pull **timestamps, short clips, and stills** for the window.
   - Join with ticket metadata (ticket #, asset, fault code, parts used if any).
   - Optional: simple computer vision cues (panel door open/closed, ladder present, technician badge in frame) to propose steps like *â€œAccessed panel,â€ â€œReset,â€ â€œReplaced component,â€ â€œVerified run.â€*

   - On Confirm/Edit, push the finalized notes back to **SIM/River** and attach the clip(s)/stills.
   - Store video **short-retention** (e.g., 30â€“60 days), notes permanent. Clips used for documentation can be retained longer under a maintenance bucket.

What is a safety in football

## 2025-08-14T21:28:54.261685Z â€” assistant
In American football, a **safety** is two things â€” a *scoring play* **and** a *defensive position*.  

**1ï¸âƒ£ Scoring Play â€” â€œThe Safetyâ€ (2 points)**  
A safety happens when the offense causes the ball to become *dead* in its own end zone. Common ways this happens:  
- The ball carrier is tackled in their own end zone.  
- The ball carrier steps out of bounds in their own end zone.  
- The offense commits a penalty in their own end zone (e.g., holding).  
- The ball goes out of bounds behind their own goal line after being last touched by them.  

Result: Defense scores **2 points** and gets the ball back via a free kick from the 20-yard line.  

**Example:**  
Quarterback drops back to pass, gets sacked in the end zone â†’ **Safety**.  

---

**2ï¸âƒ£ Defensive Position â€” â€œThe Safetyâ€ (Player role)**

- **Free Safety (FS):** Usually plays deeper, covers passes, reads the quarterback.  
- **Strong Safety (SS):** Plays closer to the line, helps stop the run, covers tight ends.
